mysql> select a.employee_id, a.fname,a.lname,a.salary,b.name,c.city from employees a,departments b,locations c where a.salary = (select max(salary) from employees where hire_date between '2002-01-01' and
'2003-12-31') and a.department_id = b.department_id and b.location_id=c.location_id;
